        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-27"/>
        3/27/2016
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This place is perfect to do a bit of reading or get some work done. Also great if you've got a friend to accompany you and you just want to talk. I went in on a sunny afternoon after lunch and ordered a Macchiato and spent hours reading and people watching -- one of my favourite urban activities. <br/><br/>I'm yet to try out their New Orleans Iced Coffee but I'm fairly sure that's what I'll have when I'm visiting next.</p>

    </div>

        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_2" title="2.0 star rating">
            <img alt="2.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2.0"/>

            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-24"/>
        3/24/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I read all of the review for Blue Bottle. &#160;I had high expectations on the service and on the product. &#160;First of all, the guy that helped me was extremely rude. &#160;I had a few questions about some of their brews, and he gave me answers that made me feel unappreciated and demeaning. &#160;<br/><br/>I ordered their cold brew, and honestly, I didn't love the coffee. &#160;The coffee is definitely more on the earthy side and I honestly did not like the coffee at all. &#160;The location is in a weird place and was a little difficult to find at first, but with a little looking around, I located the store. &#160;<br/><br/>I personally enjoy Philz coffee a lot more. &#160;If you're not into earthy coffees, I would pass on Blue Bottle.</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Oh my stars. This place is good but oh so busy!<br/>Even on a rainy rainy Sunday morning!<br/>The lines are crazy and seating is near impossible but the food is yummy and coffee beautiful.<br/><br/>I got the eggs, cauliflower and toast breakfast and a cappuccino - no complaints and my friend and I were lucky enough to nab an amazing bar seat right near the siphoning action.<br/><br/>Note to self to try the $8 siphoned coffee. &#160;We heard it's most delicious and obvi served hot to provide the best flavor. &#160;Additionally, as it cools the taste transforms. &#160;The way it's made is worth watching too. &#160;Fun! &#160;<br/><br/>You can buy beans and cookbooks as you enter and don't forget the lids are in the corner to the left, opposite the door/register. &#160;<br/><br/>--vv happy customer</p>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This is a great coffee shop located in a quiet spot of central San Francisco. The place is nicely decorated, service is quick and very friendly. The atmosphere here is very relaxed and comfortable. All the classic coffee drinks are on the menu and done professionally by the Barista. For sure they know what they are doing. Good value for money!</p>

                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-08"/>
        3/8/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This is the largest and nicest Blue Bottle location I have been to with both indoor as well as outdoor seating and some small meal items which other locations don't have.<br/>Service was nice, it was super busy so there was a bit of a wait.<br/>Prices are steep, but the quality is fantastic, I went with the mocha as always, such a great combination and they real, rich chocolate they use makes all the difference.<br/>One of the places I have to go every time I am in SF!</p>

    </div>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-01-10"/>
        1/10/2016
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This is the 2nd Blue Bottle Coffee establishment that I have been to and this one was even better than the last. It's located in the back corner of a building but you'll know you're at the right place when you see the long line of people out the door trying to get their caffeine fix.<br/><br/>I ordered the Caffe Latte and my cousins ordered the Hot Cocoa. The latte was just as good as I had hoped. Rich coffee flavor with a smooth creamy finish from the milk. Plus the art is spectacular! These baristas are pros! Somehow they are able to create art in every single cup. The hot cocoa was amazing as well! Kids may not like it because it has a dark chocolate taste to it, but I loved it! And it doesn't have that chalky feeling at the end that you normally get at Starbucks. <br/><br/>Overall, the place is nice, with more seating than the Oakland location. The location is away from the main street so you have to be in the know to find out. The coffee here is top notch plus they serve food like waffles and such. Highly recommend!</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-02-27"/>
        2/27/2016
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">As a caffeine based life-form and an avid coffee lover, I can say that this place is amazing! No scratch that, epically amazing*. From the service, to the quality of the coffee, all I can say is 'ah, perfection'. I used my 'Yelp-fu' skills to discover this place a few months ago, and I have been coming back here almost every week. The coffee beans are fresh, the food is amazing, and oh dear the affogato - is made from the tears of angels!! Wow I just drooled a little ... no one saw that.<br/><br/>Yeah the line, can be quite long. But totally worth the wait!!!<br/><br/>tldr: amazing place, worth the wait, don't fogato to order your affogato.</p>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Tried their drip coffee au lait on a rainy day and it was smooth and mellow yet strong. <br/><br/>The location itself is kind of hard to find. It's in the corner of the business building. It's neat and also busy bustling with hipsters in the morning. Like WOW I couldn't believe I was in the vicinity of so many hipsters all in one space. But I guess coffee brings beautiful people together haha</p>

            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>

            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-16"/>
        3/16/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I will keep it short and sweet: I've been all over the world, and Blue Bottle Coffee Co. has the best coffee I have ever had in my life. Nothing else compares. Skip all the espresso milk-based drinks and just get the single-origin drip coffee. Don't add any sugar or milk -- just drink it black. Trust me. You will be transcended to the next level of coffee enjoyment. <br/><br/>No need to thank me.</p>

                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-25"/>
        3/25/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">One of the best places for coffee in SF. I visit this Blue Bottle at least 1-2x a week and have never been disappointed. Latte art is beautiful and their espresso is always delicious. There is always a long line to order but the line will move fast and they make drinks fast! The burnt orange pound cake is absolutely divine! They have restrooms but ask the baristas for the key. Highly recommend stopping by for delicious espresso coffee! The next thing to try on my list is their affogato which i hear is amazing!</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-08"/>
        3/8/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Best espresso that I've found in San Francisco so far. &#160;And unfortunately, everyone and every tourist knows it. &#160;There is always a long line that extends past the door, even in the middle of a downpour. &#160;Their lattes are on point. &#160;The steamed milk has the perfect consistency which allows it to hold a beautiful latte art design and the espresso is smooth. &#160;Definitely for the purist, as there are no fancy schmancy syrups or flavored lattes. &#160;But, seriously, this latte doesn't need any sugar.<br/><br/>I have also had their famous iced New Orleans coffee which I thought was okay...sweetened and chicory-filled...but it sort of paled in comparison to their espresso drinks. &#160;I was also really intrigued that this Blue Bottle also offered siphon coffee brewing on a few of their single origin coffees. &#160;The siphon method of brewing offers a much fuller and usually lighter flavor profile. &#160;It is unique in the temperature stability which also produces some flavor notes that other brewing methods do not provide. &#160;The siphon coffee barista or sommelier (as my brother referred to him) was dedicated to just siphon brewing and was very exact in his procedure. &#160;He often used the thermometer and he also hand-delivered each brew with an explanation to the consumer. &#160;Nice touch of service! &#160;I was able to sample two of their coffees brewed this way and I was impressed with the level of attention/care given to each. &#160;The coffees were still a little on the bright side for my liking, but still enjoyable. &#160;Also you get super cute tall glass mugs to drink your siphon brew out of. &#160;A small siphon will serve about 2 cups. &#160;I do want to try their Oji brewed coffee though--the contraption used to brew this coffee definitely looked like something out of a chem lab.<br/><br/>One thing that surprised me was that they serve real food too at this location (not sure if they do this at other locations, too). &#160;But, on Saturday they offered some breakfast/brunch options. &#160;I ordered the sunny side eggs &amp; cauliflower dish which was surprisingly delicious, albeit a bit pricey. &#160;The other food options looked delicious, too and I would return to try some of their other food (if I am up for waiting in line!)<br/><br/>Really, I can't complain about anything here except that my wallet can't afford to try every single thing on the menu (even though I want to!). &#160;Wish they offered latte-making classes...and built a Blue Bottle that was large enough to support the long lines!</p>

    </div>
    <div class="review-footer clearfix">

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-25"/>
        10/25/2015
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I love this coffee shop. It's trendy, cool looking with tall ceilings and away from the street in a quiet corner. If you did not know this place existed you probably would not find it. There is no sign outside the shop and all you see the number 66 Mint outside the shop and a small Blue Bottle logo. <br/><br/>It looks like a chemistry lab on the inside with narrow long tables and some space to sit along the big old windows and look out. It's certainly not the place to sit out and people watch as there is barely anyone on this street besides people who are coming to this shop. The inside however is a whole different story....trendy people ordering coffee and eating breakfast ;-))<br/><br/>I love their coffee and whilst I am not a big fan of cold brew and so on, I always appreciate a good cuppa coffee :-) they also have a limited choice of food items and you can buy beans to take home. They use cloverleaf organic milk and the coffee has been consistently good here.</p>

                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0"/>
    </div>

            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-02-21"/>
        2/21/2016
    </span>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">It was a beautiful morning and I wanted to grab some coffee. Starbucks was the closet but I always love trying other places when I'm in the city so I decided to yelp and Blue Bottle Coffee popped up. I stayed at the Hilton in Union Square so the walk was only 5 minutes. I couldn't believe that there was a line out the door so that must mean it was good? It took me atleast 15 minutes until I got to the register and I decided to order the cafee latte. It then took atleast 10 minutes until I got my order but I didn't mind because anything for some good coffee, right? Yep, sure didn't mind because it was worth the wait! I enjoyed sipping on the yummy latte while walking and then chilling at Union Square. <br/><br/>They had a breakfast menu but I was really there for some coffee. The inside was pretty small and everyone was pretty much close to each other. It's a cool place to just order to go. Overall, I'll definitely go back again and try something else.</p>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Blue never cease to amaze me! Consistent with the quality of their coffee. I use to go to the Ferry Building location but so glad I found this one on Mint. Don't have to crowd with the tourists and great large communal table to sit and enjoy your coffee. <br/>I tried their shortbread and almond rocher and both were amazing especially with my cappuccino. What a great start to my morning! ;)<br/><br/>This place gets super busy. I'm sure that's the case for all Blue locations.</p>

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"/> 1 check-in</span>

                        <div class="review-favorites-lists">
            <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_menu_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_menu_c-common_sprite"/>     Listed in <a href="/list/caffeinated-coffee-in-cafes-san-francisco" title="I have been addicted to coffee ever since I started to go to cafe shops with Wi-Fi to be productive and get some work done!">Caffeinated Coffee In Cafes!</a>
</span>
        </div>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Blue bottle chain always find hidden gems and alleyways to locate their coffee beans at. &#160;This place is one of those spots.<br/><br/>I was meeting up with an out of city, dear friend of mine and opted for Blue bottle since it is a staple for San Francisco.<br/><br/>This coffee stop was it. &#160;It's tucked away in an alley that is not too far from central Westfield mall and offers seclusion if you want to get away from the bustling crowd. <br/><br/>Quaint surrounding and an open plaza was of existence here. &#160;Like Blue bottle coffee's aroma, the ambiance provided an urban feel to just shy yourself into. &#160;<br/><br/>Kickback and remember to smell the coffee.</p>

            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
            <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1.0"/>

            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-21"/>
        3/21/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This place doesn't deserve the hype it's getting! The lines are always long but it is not because of the quality of coffee or the food, its because of the staff who is slow and unfocused. <br/>It takes the exact amount of time to prepare espresso and their signature breakfast sandwich which is about 20-25 minutes. By the way the food is dry and flavorless and coffee is burned and bitter... Like my review. <br/>So, to sum things up, this place is the sane as any starbucks around the world, no flavor, no class and no good coffee! Avoid it at any cost!</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-03-17"/>
        3/17/2016
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">

        <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_ecac25-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_ecac25-common_sprite"/> 2 check-ins</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">So, I found this place by accident. When I stopped there was a line from the counter all the way out the door onto the sidewalk and then literally around the building. Usually, with a line like that I wouldn't even consider waiting, but as you can see from the other reviews many people believe this to be the best coffee in the world.<br/><br/>However, I did wait , and I'm glad I did because the total time from getting in line to walking out the door with my coffee with less than 10 minutes. I got my coffee faster than when I am the only customer at a Starbucks.<br/><br/>As for the coffee itself - I ordered the Frozen New Orleans coffee , and while I cannot comfortably saying that it was the best coffee in the world, I also can't think of a time I've tasted better coffee.<br/><br/>So yes, wait in line, it won't be that bad , if anything you'll at least get a great cup of coffee at a fair price.</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0"/>
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-01-10"/>
        1/10/2016
    </span>

    </div>


                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I ordered a siphon which was really good and got me going in the morning ...I am from LA and they only have their blend for some reason so it was definitely a positive experience being able to try a single origin coffee<br/>I also had a bread with poached eggs with a side of marmalade which was really delicious.<br/>Recommend also trying their hot chocolate..one of the best I've had in California</p>
